** BELGIUM AND LUXEMBOURG AIRSPACE
** BY DAY ON WEEKDAYS WHEN MILITARY ARE ACTIVE
** LAST UPDATED 02 MAY 2020
*******************************************************************
* FILE DOES NOT CONTAIN AIRSPACE ABOVE FL95
* FILE DOES NOT CONTAIN AIRSPACE ABOVE THE SEA
* FILE DOES NOT CONTAIN AIRSPACE ACTIVE ONLY AT NIGHT
* FILE DOES NOT CONTAIN AIRWAYS
* FILE DOES NOT CONTAIN MOST WARNING AREAS FOR 
* BALLOON/GLIDER/MODEL OPS
* RESTRICTED AREAS ARE SHOWN AS PROHIBITED AREAS IF ENTRY IS
* PERMANENTLY PROHIBITED TO ALL GENERAL AVIATION AIRCRAFT

*	- MEEUWEN PARA NEW POSITION
*	- LEOPOLDSBURG PARA NOW 3 NM
*	- NOERTANGE PARA ADAPTED
*	- OUD-TURNHOUT PARA NOT MAINTAINED, BECAUSE AFD CLOSED, ALTHOUGH STATED IN AIP
*	- AIRSPACE ABOVE LFA G1 & G2 CONSIDERED AS BRUSSELS LCA CLASS C
*--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
* CLASS G AIRSPACE AREA LFA GOLF 1 IS PERMANENTLY ACTIVE DURING SAT/SUN/HOLIDAY - EXCEPT BY NOTAM
* AIRSPACE AREAS LFA GOLF 2 NORTH, SOUTH AND WEST, AND LFA GOLF 5, ARE DEFINED AS C-CLASS AREAS AND WILL THUS TRIGGER AN AIRSPACE WARNING WITH SEEYOU MOBILE AND WINPILOT OR SIMILAR.
* THE SAME APPLIES FOR GLIDER SECTORS LFA GOLF 4 (GOETSENHOVEN) AND OVERBOELARE
* PILOTS HAVE TO DEACTIVATE (SWITCH OFF) THESE AREAS WHEN CLEARED FOR GLIDER FLYING ! ! ! !
* AIRSPACE LFA GOLF 3 (VERVIERS AREA) IS DEFINED AS W-CLASS AREA ONLY: IF GOLF 2 SOUTH IS NOT ACTIVE, THIS WILL PROBABLY TRIGGER AN ALARM ABOVE FL50
***************************************************************

* ! ! ! ! ONLY FOR USE AT OWN RISK - NO LIABILITY ACCEPTED ! ! ! ! !
